(function() {

	var branding = {
			padTop:130,
			bgColor:'#fff',
			fixed:true,
			hwAlco:false,
			hwMed:false,
			iuaNew:false
		};
	
	function addEvent(e,t,f) {
		if (e.addEventListener) {
			e.addEventListener(t, f, false);
		} else if (e.attachEvent) {
			e.attachEvent('on'+t, f);
		}
	}
	
	function removeEvent(e,t,f) {
		if (e.removeEventListener) {
			e.removeEventListener(t, f, false);
		} else if (e.detachEvent) {
			e.detachEvent('on'+t, f);
		}
	}
	
	function merge() {
		var options, name, copy, target=arguments[0] || {};
		for (i = 1; i < arguments.length; i++ )
			if ((options = arguments[i]) != null)
				for (name in options)
					if (options.hasOwnProperty(name) && options[name] !== undefined)
						target[name] = options[name];
		return target;
	}

	function GEBCN(cn){
		if(document.getElementsByClassName) // Returns NodeList here
			return document.getElementsByClassName(cn);

		cn = cn.replace(/ *$/, '');

		if(document.querySelectorAll) // Returns NodeList here
			return document.querySelectorAll((' ' + cn).replace(/ +/g, '.'));

		cn = cn.replace(/^ */, '');

		var classes = cn.split(/ +/), clength = classes.length;
		var els = document.getElementsByTagName('*'), elength = els.length;
		var results = [];
		var i, j, match;

		for(i = 0; i < elength; i++){
			match = true;
			for(j = clength; j--;)
				if(!RegExp(' ' + classes[j] + ' ').test(' ' + els[i].className + ' '))
					match = false;
			if(match)
				results.push(els[i]);
		}

		// Returns Array here
		return results;
	}

	function addClass (o, c) {
		var re = new RegExp("(^|\\s)" + c + "(\\s|$)", "g");
		if (re.test(o.className)) return
		o.className = (o.className + " " + c).replace(/\s+/g, " ").replace(/(^ | $)/g, "");
	}

	function getStyle(e,s){
		if (e.currentStyle) { return e.currentStyle[s]||''; }
		else if (window.getComputedStyle) { return window.getComputedStyle(e,null)[s]||''; }
	}

	addEvent(window,"message", catchMsg);
	
	function catchMsg(e) {
		if (typeof e.data == 'string') {
			var str = e.data;
			if (str.indexOf('admBranding_padTop') != -1) {
				branding.padTop = str.split('_')[str.split('_').length-1]; 
			}
			if (str.indexOf('admBranding_bgColor') != -1) {
				branding.bgColor = str.split('_')[str.split('_').length-1];
			}
			if (str.indexOf('admBranding_fixed') != -1) {
				branding.fixed = str.split('_')[str.split('_').length-1];
			}
			if (str.indexOf('admBranding_hwAlco') != -1) {
				branding.hwAlco = str.split('_')[str.split('_').length-1];
				branding.hwAlco = (branding.hwAlco=='true')?true:false;
			}
			if (str.indexOf('admBranding_hwMed') != -1) {
				branding.hwMed = str.split('_')[str.split('_').length-1];
				branding.hwMed = (branding.hwMed=='true')?true:false;
			}
			if (str.indexOf('admBranding_iuaNew') != -1) {
				branding.iuaNew = str.split('_')[str.split('_').length-1];
				branding.iuaNew = (branding.iuaNew=='true')?true:false;
			}
			if (e.data == 'admix_branding') {
				loadBranding();
				removeEvent(window,"message", catchMsg);
			}
		}
	}

					'admixer_top_kino',  // kino
					'admixer_top_inner'];  // inner
					
		for (var i=0; i<topId.length; i++) {
			if (document.getElementById(topId[i])) {
				html_brnd = document.getElementById(topId[i]);
				break;
			}
		}
		
		var partition = window.location.hostname.split('.')[0];
		
		if (branding.iuaNew) {

			var partitions_new = ['weather','finance','perevod','map','tv','goroskop','prikol'];
			
			var isNewPartition = (function() {
				for (var i=0; i < partitions_new.length; i++) {
					if (partitions_new[i] == partition) {
						return true;
					}
				}
				return false;
			})();
			
			if (isNewPartition) {
				
				var bOffset = 47;
				
				if (html_brnd) {
					if (html_brnd.firstChild) {
						html_brnd_first = html_brnd.firstChild;
						merge(html_brnd_first.style, {'max-width':'100%','max-height':'100%','min-width':'100%','min-height':'100%'});
					}
				} else {
					console.log('Function loadBranding stopped');
					console.log('Place holder id for TOP banner is not found in topId array');
					return;
				}
				
				if (typeof I_VER3 !== 'undefined') {
					
					if (GEBCN('body_container')[0]) {
						var body_cont = GEBCN('body_container')[0];
					}
					
					addClass(document.body, 'iua_branding');
					document.body.style.overflowX = 'hidden';
					
					if (GEBCN('header_adv')[0]) {
						var header_adv_cont = GEBCN('header_adv')[0];
						header_adv_cont.style.display = 'none';
					}
					
					if (GEBCN('header_container').length) {
						merge(GEBCN('header_container')[0].style, {'position':'absolute','width':'100%','z-index':2});
					}
					
					if (GEBCN('page')[0]) {
						var page_cont = GEBCN('page')[0];
						merge(page_cont.style, {'position':'relative','z-index':1});
						var contWidth = getStyle(page_cont, 'width'); 
						if (~contWidth.indexOf("px")) {
							contWidth = +contWidth.slice(0,contWidth.length-2)+8;
						}
					}
					
					body_cont.style.top = (bOffset+parseInt(branding.padTop)) + 'px';
					
					if (document.getElementById('section_nav')) {
						document.getElementById('section_nav').style.zIndex = 1;
					}
					
					if (GEBCN('footer_container').length) {
						merge(GEBCN('footer_container')[0].style, {'top':parseInt(branding.padTop)+20+ 'px', 'z-index':1});
					}
					
					merge(html_brnd.style, {'position':'fixed','top':bOffset+'px','width':'100%','height':'100%','overflow': 'hidden','z-index':0});
					document.body.appendChild(html_brnd);
					
					$(window).scroll(function () {
						if ($(window).scrollTop() >= bOffset) {
							$(html_brnd).css({'top':0+'px', 'position':'fixed'});
						} else {
							$(html_brnd).css({'top':bOffset-$(window).scrollTop()+'px', 'position':'absolute'});
						}
					});
					
					function addHealthWarning() {
						var hwDiv = document.createElement('DIV');
						GEBCN('page')[0].appendChild(hwDiv);
						merge(hwDiv.style, {
							'position':'relative',
							'width':'1100px',
							'height':'142px',
							'margin':'0 auto',
							'min-width':'1100px',
							'max-width':'1100px',
							'background-color':'#fff',
							'background-image': (branding.hwAlco ? 'url(//i.holder.com.ua/h/1/2/282_pf2_1.jpg)' : branding.hwMed ? 'url(//i.holder.com.ua/h/5/6/266_pf1_1.jpg)' : ''),
							'background-repeat':'no-repeat',
							'background-position':'center top',
							'background-size':'contain',
							'z-index':1
						});
						
					}
					
					if (branding.hwAlco || branding.hwMed) {
						addHealthWarning();
					}
						
				}
					
			}
				
		} else {
				
			if (html_brnd) {
				if (html_brnd.firstChild) {
					html_brnd_first = html_brnd.firstChild;
					merge(html_brnd_first.style, {'max-width':'100%','max-height':'150px','min-width':'100%','min-height':'150px'});
				}
			} else {
				console.log('Function loadBranding stopped');
				console.log('Place holder id for TOP banner is not found in topId array');
				return;
			}
			
			merge(html_brnd.style, {'width':'100%','height':'150px','max-width':'100%','max-height':'150px','min-width':'100%','min-height':'150px','margin':'0px auto'});
			if (GEBCN('header_adv').length) {
				GEBCN('header_adv')[0].style.padding = '0px';
			}
			if (GEBCN('header_adv_item').length) {
				merge(GEBCN('header_adv_item')[0].style, { 'width':'100%', 'border':'none' });
			}
			if (GEBCN('widget_adv').length) {
				merge(GEBCN('widget_adv')[0].style, { 'width':'100%', 'border':'none' });
			}
			
		}
		
	}
})();
</script><script type="text/javascript">

        log: 'disabled' !== 'disabled',
        placementID: 2483,
        gaTrackingID: '',
      },
    };

    var interval = setInterval(function() {
      if (!window.IMA || !window.Moxplayer) return;

      clearInterval(interval);

      var ima = new window.IMA(imaConfig);

      ima.once('loaded', function(event) {
        var playback = ima.getPlayback();

        var trackedEvents = ['AdLoaded', 'AdStarted', 'AdClickThru', 'AdError'];
        var completeEvents = ['AdVideoComplete', 'AdSkipped', 'AdStopped'];

        playback.on(trackedEvents, function(event) {
          var eventName = event.getName();
          var eventData = null;

          if (eventName === 'AdStarted') {
            setTimeout(function() {
              eventName = 'AdProgress';
              eventData = {elapsed: 3000};

              emit(eventName, eventData);
            }, 3000);

            eventData = playback._activeAd.getDimensions();
          } else if (eventName === 'AdClickThru') {
            eventData = {url: event.getData().url};
          }

          emit(eventName, eventData);
        });

        playback.once(completeEvents, emit.bind(null, 'AdComplete', null));
      });
    }, 50);

    var emit = function(eventName, eventData) {
      try {
        var message = {
          provider: 'moxtv',
          event: {
            id: '2483',
            name: eventName,
            data: eventData,
          },
        };

        var target = window;

        while (target) {
          target.postMessage(message, '*');

          target = target === window.top ? null : target.parent;
        }
      } catch (e) {
        // ..
      }
    };

    imaConfig.playback.strategy['' === 'enabled' ? 'multiThread' : 'linear'] = {
      maxRotations: '1' || '1',
    };

    if ('' === 'inViewport') {
      imaConfig.adSlot.placement.position = {
        inViewport: {
          beforeChild: '' || 'last',
        },
      };
    } else {
      imaConfig.adSlot.placement.position = {
        constant: {
          beforeChild: '' || 0,
        },
      };
    }

    switch ('slider') {
      case 'slider': {
        imaConfig.adSlot.stage.mainAxis = 'vertical';
        imaConfig.adSlot.stage.properties.fixed = {
          position: ('left' || 'right') + ' ' + ('bottom' || 'bottom'),
          margin: ['' || '0', '' || '0'],
        };

        break;
      }
      case 'inBanner': {
        imaConfig.adSlot.stage.properties.filled = {color: '#000'};
        imaConfig.adSlot.stage.properties.stretched = {};
      }
      case 'richVideo': {
        imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.states.initial = 'expanded';
        imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.states.final = 'expanded';

        break;
      }
      default: {
        // ..
      }
    }

    if ('' !== '') {
      imaConfig.adSlot.stage.properties.filled = {color: '#000'};
      imaConfig.adSlot.stage.properties.parallax = {
        initialOffset: 'px',
      };
    }

    if ('onReady' === 'inViewport') {
      imaConfig.playback.ad.strategies.resolveVASTAdTag = {
        inViewport: {
          offset: '500' || '-100',
        },
      };
    } else {
      imaConfig.playback.ad.strategies.resolveVASTAdTag = {onReady: {}};
    }

    if ('onReady' === 'inViewport') {
      imaConfig.playback.ad.strategies.startAd = {
        inViewport: {
          offset: '200' || '-50%',
        },
      };
    } else {
      imaConfig.playback.ad.strategies.startAd = {onReady: {}};
    }

    if ('onHover' === 'onReady') {
      imaConfig.playback.ad.strategies.volume = {
        onReady: {
          level: '0.2' || '0.4',
          transition: {
            type: 'smooth',
            duration: 1.5,
          },
        },
      };
    } else {
      imaConfig.playback.ad.strategies.volume = {
        onHover: {
          level: '0.2' || '0.4',
          transition: {
            type: 'smooth',
            duration: 1.5,
          },
        },
      };
    }

    if ('enabled' !== 'disabled') {
      imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.controls.volume = {
        size: 20,
        margin: 10,
        position: 'left bottom',
      };
    }

    // if ('disabled' === 'enabled') {
    //   imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.brandIcon = {
    //     position: ('left' || 'left') + ' ' + ('top' || 'top'),
    //     outside: 'outside' !== 'inside',
    //     url: 'https://mox.tv/?utm_source=mox.tv_branding',
    //   };
    // }

    if ('enabled' === 'enabled') {
      imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.caption = {
        position: ('center' || 'center') + ' ' + ('top' || 'top'),
        outside: 'outside' !== 'inside',
        text: 'advertisement',
      };
    }

    switch ('30') {
      case '10': {
        if (imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.brandIcon) {
          imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.brandIcon.height = 10;
          imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.brandIcon.margin = 3;
        }
        if (imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.caption) {
          imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.caption.fontSize = 10;
          imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.caption.margin = 3;
        }
        if (imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.controls.close) {
          imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.controls.close.size = 10;
          imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.controls.close.margin = 2;
        }

        break;
      }
      case '30': {
        if (imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.brandIcon) {
          imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.brandIcon.height = 20;
          imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.brandIcon.margin = 5;
        }
        if (imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.caption) {
          imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.caption.fontSize = 15;
          imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.caption.margin = 5;
        }
        if (imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.controls.close) {
          imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.controls.close.size = 30;
          imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.controls.close.margin = 6;
        }

        break;
      }
      default: {
        if (imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.brandIcon) {
          imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.brandIcon.height = 15;
          imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.brandIcon.margin = 5.5;
        }
        if (imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.caption) {
          imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.caption.fontSize = 12;
          imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.caption.margin = 5;
        }
        if (imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.controls.close) {
          imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.controls.close.size = 20;
          imaConfig.adSlot.stage.proscenium.uiElements.controls.close.margin = 2;
        }
      }
    }

    if ('disabled' === 'enabled') {
      imaConfig.adSlot.stage.properties.sticky = {
        condition: function() {
          return '' !== 'disabled' && window.innerWidth >= 350;
        },
        reconfigure: {
          adSlot: {
            stage: {
              proscenium: {
                maxDimensions: {
                   width: 320,
                   height: 180,
                 // width: 400,
                 // height: 300,
                },
                uiElements: {
                  controls: {
                  close: {
                      size: 20,
                      margin: 2,
                      outside: false,
                      visible: true,
                    },
                    volume: {size: 17},
                  },
                  // brandIcon: {
                  //   height: 10,
                  //   margin: 3,
                  //   outside: false,
                  // },
                  caption: {
                    fontSize: 10,
                    margin: 3,
                    outside: false,
                  },
                },
              },
              properties: {
                fixed: {
                  position: ('' || 'right') + ' ' + ('' || 'bottom'),
                  margin: ['', ''],
                },
              },
            },
          },
        },
        offset: '-10%',
      };
    }

    try {
      if (!~window.top.location.hash.indexOf('x_preview')) return;

      // var tag = 'https://ad.mox.tv/delivery/video/zona/3457?video=vast&pzoneid=3457';
      var tag = 'https://pubads.g.doubleclick.net/gampad/ads?sz=640x480&iu=/124319096/external/single_ad_samples&ciu_szs=300x250&impl=s&gdfp_req=1&env=vp&output=vast&unviewed_position_start=1&cust_params=deployment%3Ddevsite%26sample_ct%3Dskippablelinear&correlator=16004954345f659f4a8c4f9';
      var action = ~window.top.location.hash.indexOf('forced') ? 'unshift' : 'push';

      imaConfig.playback.tags.pre.passbacks[action](tag);
    } catch (e) {
		//...
    }

  }(window));
</script>

function showColumn(obj) {
	if (obj.className=='close')
	{
		obj.className='open';
		obj.parentNode.className='width1p';
		cells = obj.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('td');
		for (i=0; i<cells.length; i++) if (cells[i] == obj.parentNode) curCell = i;

		rows = obj.parentNode.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('tr');
		for (i=1; i<rows.length; i++)
		{
			cells = rows[i].getElementsByTagName('td');
			cells[curCell].childNodes[0].style.display='none';
		}
	}
	else {
		obj.className='close';
		obj.parentNode.className='width25p';
		cells = obj.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('td');
		for (i=0; i<cells.length; i++) if (cells[i] == obj.parentNode) curCell = i;

		rows = obj.parentNode.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('tr');
		for (i=1; i<rows.length; i++)
		{
			cells = rows[i].getElementsByTagName('td');
			cells[curCell].childNodes[0].style.display='';
		}
	}
	utilSetCookie(obj.getAttribute('name'), obj.className, new Date(1915855433*1000));
}
